{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int get\+Next\+Id (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{expr,  }\item[{int}]{p,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{l }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

returns the next identifier in string {\itshape expr} by starting at position {\itshape p}. The position of the identifier is returned (or -\/1 if nothing is found) and {\itshape l} is its length. Any quoted strings are skipping during the search.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{processUntilMatchingTerminator()}{processUntilMatchingTerminator()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static const char $\ast$ process\+Until\+Matching\+Terminator (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{input\+Str,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{result }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Process string or character literal. 

{\itshape input\+Str} should point to the start of a string or character literal. the routine will return a pointer to just after the end of the literal the character making up the literal will be added to {\itshape result}. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2pre_8l_source_l02717}{2717}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2pre_8l_source}{pre.\+l}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{replaceFunctionMacro()}{replaceFunctionMacro()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static bool replace\+Function\+Macro (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2code_8l_a9484188abbc459dafcbd4c96425fa70b}{yyscan\+\_\+t}}}]{yyscanner,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{expr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} $\ast$}]{rest,  }\item[{int}]{pos,  }\item[{int \&}]{len,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_define}{Define}} $\ast$}]{def,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{result,  }\item[{int}]{level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

replaces the function macro {\itshape def} whose argument list starts at {\itshape pos} in expression {\itshape expr}. Notice that this routine may scan beyond the {\itshape expr} string if needed. In that case the characters will be read from the input file. The replacement string will be returned in {\itshape result} and the length of the (unexpanded) argument list is stored in {\itshape len}. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2pre_8l_source_l02249}{2249}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2pre_8l_source}{pre.\+l}}.
